Simplify your site visits with the most powerful drafting and editing tool available. \r\n\r\nThe AutoCAD mobile app offers an abundance of features and capabilities. Upload and open 2D DWG drawings directly from hard disk drive, email or external storage and view all aspects of your DWG file, including external references, layers, and image underlays.
